# Resumo Clínico — Por Favor Leia Antes de Avaliar (2026)

**Tipo:** Documento auto-preparado para apresentação em urgências
**Paciente:** Patient

---

## Verbatim Transcription

**RESUMO CLÍNICO — POR FAVOR LEIA ANTES DE AVALIAR**

**Nome:** Patient **DN:** [DOB REMOVED] | **Sexo:** M | **Nº Doente CUF:** [ID REMOVED]

**Diagnósticos conhecidos:** Perturbação afetiva bipolar (estável, seguido em psiquiatria) Apneia obstrutiva do sono (AHI 7, em CPAP) Disfunção autonómica em estudo (em seguimento com [Cardiologista B (Porto)], Hospital A (Porto)) Defeito de concentração renal associado a lítio (poliúria documentada ~4350ml/24h e ~5500ml/24h)

**Medicação atual:** Lítio 600mg | Quetiapina 50mg

**O que se passa comigo:** Tenho suspeita em investigação de uma doença do sistema nervoso autónomo em investigação desde 2024. Desde então, tenho tido sintomas progressivos como fadiga crónica, poliúria, perda de sensação e vários sintomas neurológicos que vão aparecendo ao longo do tempo.

Estou a ser seguido pelo [Cardiologista B (Porto)] (cardiologia autonómica, Hospital A (Porto)), que já pediu prova de esforço e teste de tilt table. Tenho também seguimento em psiquiatria ([Psiquiatra B (Porto)], [Clínica Psiquiatria A (Porto)]), nefrologia ([Nefrologista A (Porto)], [Clínica Nefrologia A]), e uma avaliação de cardiologia em Londres ([Cardiologista A (London)]).

**Nota sobre movimentos involuntários:** Tenho história de distonia / parkinsonismo medicamentosa documentada em novembro de 2022 no Hospital A (Porto) e pelo meu psiquiatra. Foi atribuída à medicação (quetiapina 300mg + lamotrigina) e tratada com Artane. Se apresentar estereotipias ou movimentos involuntários, estes são consistentes com esse antecedente — não com intoxicação ou uso de substâncias.

**Indico por favor:** Que sintomas neurológicos sejam avaliados como tal, independentemente do meu diagnóstico psiquiátrico. A minha doença bipolar está controlada. O nível de lítio pode aparecer baixo (<0.20-0.42) devido ao defeito renal de concentração documentado — não por falta de adesão à medicação.

**Contacto dos meus médicos assistentes:** [Cardiologista B (Porto)] — Hospital A (Porto), Cardiologia / Função Autonómica e [Psiquiatra B (Porto)], [Clínica Psiquiatria A (Porto)].

---

> **English translation note:**
>
> **Clinical Summary — Please Read Before Assessing**
>
> Self-prepared document for emergency presentations. Key points:
> - Known diagnoses: Bipolar disorder (stable), OSA (AHI 7, on CPAP), autonomic dysfunction under investigation, lithium-related renal concentrating defect (documented polyuria ~4350-5500ml/24h)
> - Current meds: Lithium 600mg, Quetiapine 50mg
> - Under investigation for autonomic nervous system disease since 2024 with progressive symptoms
> - History of documented drug-induced dystonia/parkinsonism (Nov 2022) — involuntary movements are consistent with this, not intoxication
> - Requests neurological symptoms be assessed independently of psychiatric diagnosis
> - Low lithium levels (<0.20-0.42) are due to renal concentrating defect, not non-compliance

# Medical Records Index

Anonymised transcripts of medical records (2018–2026) for a patient with post-vaccine neurological, vascular, and autonomic symptoms beginning August 2021.

All documents are verbatim transcriptions in the original language (mostly Portuguese), with English translation notes included. Personal identifiers have been replaced with role-based codes (e.g. "Hospital A (Porto)", "Neurologista A (Porto)").

# Health-LLM — Project Index

An Obsidian vault documenting the medical history of a patient. Designed to be read by both humans and LLM assistants to help with diagnosis of an unknown neurological disease.
## Give this to your LLM 

- [Exhaustive File Index](exhaustiveindex.md) — Every single file in the repository with descriptions. If you are giving this project to an LLM have it start here. 
- [Basic Patient Facts](Basic%20Facts.md) — Key patient background information
#### Readme 

- [README.md](README.md) — Project description

# How to Start 

To start with try this command 

*See this website - [https://sprafa.github.io/Health-LLM-Public/exhaustiveindex.html](https://sprafa.github.io/Health-LLM-Public/exhaustiveindex.html) can you see this and [https://sprafa.github.io/Health-LLM-Public/index.html](https://sprafa.github.io/Health-LLM-Public/index.html)this should be an exhaustive list of the infomation on this website and its webpages. id like you to read them all first please. divide it into sections. go section by section. Give me a full assessment of what is in there please.* 

Make sure it read all of it. Ask it multiple times until you get a firm "Yes" that its read it all. 

Then (ideally with Deep Research/Research mode activated): 

*Do some research. What could be causing the patients symptoms?* 

And if thats inconclusive, add the Unindexed Files folder to your LLM and ask it to take those into consideration either as project files or message attachment. You can attach them to any message to ChatGPT or Claude as additional information.
The Unindexed files are removed from the main repo index to prevent "guiding" the LLMs towards any preferred pathway. Think of it as a form of redteaming. This vault is supposed to help me find answers, not help me get the answer I want from others. Hence I leave the Unindexed Files as an aid if you find the LLMs answers inconclusive. ChatGPT seems particularly prone to this. Claude is more conclusive and arrives at ideas faster. 

---
# Important Start Notes and Current Observations

- I definitely have Bipolar
- Even after consistent salt loading, the condition is not stable. 
- Cauda equina like symptoms come and go (very odd)
- As of April 2026, on a stable dose of electrolytes and salt (2x bags of Dioralyte a day and +6 grams of salt a day in 600ml of water), fatigue symptoms seem to have become worse, not stable. In the UK 2x Liquid IV daily seemed to work better than Dioralyte. 
- Two major dystonia/parkinsonism/functional neurological motor symptom crisis - one in 2022 and another one in 2026. In 2022 I was on a combination of 300mg Seroquel SR or quetiapine and 50mg Lamictal. In 2026 I was on 600mg of lithium and had just tapered off quetiapine, which had been at 100mg or 50mg for years (since 2022). 
- Paresthesia is a recurring symptom. It happened in 2021 and returned in force in 2026. I had it very strongly alongside the first new motor symptom crisis in 2026. Then again when the cauda equina symptoms showed up. And they still remain to this day. 
- Loss of sensation in upper arms particularly in upper right arm is a common symptom. If I sleep on an arm, I might lose sensation on it for several minutes, which is pretty scary. I try to avoid this now. 


---
# What this Project Contains 
## Anonymised Medical Transcripts

Verbatim transcriptions of medical records (2018–2026), in original language (mostly Portuguese) with English translation notes. All personal identifiers replaced with role-based codes.

Full listing: [index of anonymised transcripts of medical records](Transcripts%20Anonymous/index%20of%20anonymised%20transcripts%20of%20medical%20records.md)

### Important Exams noted 
### 2018
- CT of the Brain done in 2018-02-27 — Brain CT scan done at onset of Bipolar. Baseline 

### 2021 — Post-vaccine onset (27 files)
- **Discharge Notes:** 5 ER discharges (Aug–Nov)
- **Lab Results:** 14 sets — D-dimer monitoring, CBC, cardiac markers, coagulation, COVID tests
- **Imaging:** 7 reports — chest/cerebral CT angio, brain MRI with spectroscopy, cervical MRI, neck CT, chest X-ray
- **Prescriptions:** 4 imaging requests
- **Psychiatry:** 1 post-vaccine GP letter
- **Reference:** 1 personal treatment protocol note

### 2022 — Continued investigations (23 files)
- **Sleep Study:** polygraphy + polysomnography data
- **Discharge Notes:** 5 ER discharges (Apr–Nov)
- **Lab Results:** 8 sets — hospital labs, cardiac markers, COVID tests
- **Imaging:** 3 reports — abdominal ultrasound, brain MRI, brain CT
- **Endoscopy:** upper endoscopy (EGD) + colonoscopy
- **Pathology:** 2 IPATIMUP biopsies (duodenal + gastric)
- **Psychiatry:** 1 final discharge letter with treatment alternatives

### 2023–2024 — Monitoring (6 files)
- Lab results: lithium, OGTT, renal panel, general labs, HbA1c

### 2025 — Escalation (5 files)
- Lab results: general labs, calcium + PTH, calcium + vitamin D

### 2026 — Active investigation (20 files)
- **Lab Results:** 7 sets — endocrine panel, protein/tryptase/ANA, lithium, cortisol/complement, ER labs
- **Cardiology:** 3 letters — dysautonomia impression, Portuguese translation, neurologist referral
- **Cardiology Tests:** exercise stress test ECG (diminished capacity)
- **Neurology:** FND diagnosis letter, normal neuro exam
- **Psychiatry:** clinical summary for ER + email clarification
- **Endocrinology:** comprehensive test request list
- **Health Log:** fatigue and dystonia diary 2024–2026
- **Prescriptions:** psychiatrist test request
